Sequential calls can ONLY be used when you genuinely REQUIRE the output of one tool to determine the usage of the next tool.\n\nDEFAULT TO PARALLEL: Unless you have a specific reason why operations MUST be sequential (output of A required for input of B), always execute multiple tools simultaneously. This is not just an optimization - it's the expected behavior. authentication schemes\n- **Core component attribute definitions**: When describing properties, types, default values, and behaviors of key UI components, services, or configuration objects\n- **Database table schemas**: When outlining tables, columns, data types, constraints (PK, FK, unique), indexes, and relationships between entities\n- **Configuration options**: When listing environment variables, feature flags, or system settings with descriptions, valid values, and scope\n- **State or enum definitions**: When clarifying possible states, status codes, or enumerated values used across the system\n- **Input/output specifications**: When defining the structure of data inputs (forms, payloads) or expected outputs (reports, responses) for clarity and validation\n- **Migration or version changes**: When comparing changes across versions, such as deprecated fields, added endpoints, or schema evolution\n\n## 7. Error\"]\n    DBResult --\u003e|Yes| ProcessData[\"Process Raw Data\"]\n    ProcessData --\u003e UpdateCache[\"Update Cache\"]\n    UpdateCache --\u003e ReturnResult[\"Return Processed Result\"]\n    HandleError --\u003e ReturnError\n    ReturnCache --\u003e End([Function Exit])\n    ReturnResult --\u003e End\n    ReturnError --\u003e End\n```\n\n## Architecture Diagrams\n```mermaid\ngraph TB\n uuid id PK\n    string name\n    string description\n    uuid owner_id FK\n    timestamp created_at\n    timestamp updated_at\n    enum status\n  }\n\n  TASK {\n    uuid id PK\n    string title\n    text description\n    uuid project_id FK\n    uuid assignee_id FK\n    timestamp due_date\n    enum priority\n    enum status\n  }\n\n  USER ||--o{ PROJECT : owns\n  USER ||--o{ TASK : assigned_to\n  PROJECT ||--o{ TASK : contains\n```\n\n## Common Mermaid Syntax Errors to Avoid:\n\n### WRONG - Custom Colors and Styling\n```\nclassDiagram\n    class User {\n        name: string\n    }\n  A[Complex Label With Spaces] --\u003e B\n```\n\n### CORRECT - Quoted Labels\n```mermaid\nflowchart TD\n    A[\"Complex Label With Spaces\"] --\u003e B[\"Another Label\"]\n```\n\n# FINAL DOCUMENT [Appendices](#appendices)\n\n## Introduction\nThis document explains the core section components that define the event websiteâ€™s primary content flow. It covers how each section consumes data from the centralized event data source and uses translation via the LanguageContext provider. It also describes responsive layout techniques using Tailwind CSS, common issues such as content overflow and image loading, accessibility considerations, and best practices for extending the template for future events.\n\n## Project Structure\nThe event website is organized around a set of dedicated section components rendered in sequence on the home page. The global language and translation system is provided by a context provider, and each section uses the t() function to render localized content. The event data is centralized in a single data module consumed by sections and the navigation.\n\n```mermaid\ngraph TB\n  subgraph \"Application Shell\"\n    App[\"App.tsx\"]\n component follows a consistent pattern:\n- Consume the LanguageContext via the useLanguage hook to access t() and language.\n- Render localized content using translation keys.\n- Use Tailwind classes for responsive layouts (grid, flex, spacing).\n- Reference assets and constants where applicable.\n\nKey data sources:\n- Centralized event data is defined in a single module and consumed by sections.\n- Translation keys are defined in the LanguageContext and mapped per language.\n\nResponsive layout techniques:\n- Grid-based cards for Goals, Agenda, Speakers, and Details.\n- Flexbox for alignment and centering.\n- Container-based max widths and auto margins for centering content.\n- Responsive breakpoints (sm, md, lg) to adapt to screen sizes.\n\nAccessibility:\n- Alt text on images.\n- Semantic headings and landmarks.\n- Focus-visible styles via Tailwind utilities.\n- Proper contrast and color roles.\n\nCommon issues and mitigations:\n- Content overflow: constrained containers and max-widths; overflow-hidden on sections where needed.\n- Image loading: lazy loading via asset imports; fallback placeholders; object-fit utilities.\n- Accessibility: aria-labels for links; semantic HTML; color contrast checks.\n\nBest practices for extension:\n- Add new translation keys to LanguageContext.\n- Extend eventData with new fields and map them in sections.\n- Reuse shared UI components (e.g., Button) for CTAs.\n- Keep responsive patterns consistent across sections.\n\n**Section sources**\n- [utils.ts](file://src/lib/utils.ts#L1-L7)\n\n## Architecture Overview\nThe sections are composed in a linear flow on the home page. Considerations\n- Asset imports: Images are bundled with the build; ensure appropriate sizes and formats for fast loading.\n- Animations: Keep the number of animated confetti pieces reasonable to avoid jank.\n- Grid layouts: Prefer CSS Grid for complex layouts; avoid excessive reflows by minimizing dynamic content inside grids.\n- Lazy loading: For large image galleries, consider lazy loading strategies; for current assets, rely on bundling.\n- Font rendering: The app switches fonts based on language; ensure font weights and fallbacks are configured.\n\n[No sources needed since this section provides general guidance]\n\n## Troubleshooting Guide\n- Content overflow:\n  - Use container utilities and max-width constraints.\n  - Apply overflow-hidden on parent containers when necessary.\n- Image loading:\n  - Ensure alt attributes are present for accessibility.\n  - Use object-fit utilities for consistent cropping.\n- Accessibility:\n  - Verify ARIA labels for external links.\n  - Confirm keyboard focus visibility.\n- Localization:\n  - Ensure translation keys exist for all languages.\n  - Validate that language switching updates all sections.\n\n**Section
